.trading.simulator import SimulatedTrader\n    37→from .trading.metrics import evaluate_predictions\n    38→\n    39→\n    40→class TradingSystem:\n    41→    \"\"\"\n    42→    Main trading system class that orchestrates the full workflow.\n    43→    \"\"\"\n    44→\n    45→    def __init__(\n    46→        self,\n    47→        data_path: str = None,\n    48→        results_dir: str = self.results_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    56→        self.log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    57→\n    58→        # Current state\n    59→        self.df = None\n    60→        self.feature_names = []\n    61→        self.main_population = None\n    62→        self.horizon_ensemble = None\n    63→        self.consensus_gate = None\n    64→        self.validator = None\n all system components.\"\"\"\n    72→        self.validator = WalkForwardValidator(\n    73→            train_days=ValidationConfig.TRAIN_DAYS,\n    74→            valid_days=ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS,\n    75→            step_days=ValidationConfig.STEP_DAYS,\n    76→            min_train_samples=ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES\n    77→        )\n    78→\n    79→        self.trader = SimulatedTrader(\n    80→            initial_capital=TradingConfig.INITIAL_CAPITAL,\n    81→            fee_rate=TradingConfig.FEE_RATE,\n    82→            slippage=TradingConfig.SLIPPAGE,\n    83→            bet_size=TradingConfig.POSITION_SIZE,\n    84→            stop_loss_pct=TradingConfig.STOP_LOSS_PCT\n    85→        )\n    86→\n    87→        self.horizon_ensemble = HorizonEnsemble(horizons=FeatureConfig.HORIZONS)\n    88→        self.consensus_gate = ConsensusGate(\n    89→            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n    90→            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    91→        )\n    92→\n    93→    def load_or_fetch_data(self, force_refetch: bool = False) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    94→        \"\"\"\n    95→        Load data from disk or fetch from Binance if not available/forced.\n    96→        \"\"\"\n    97→        if not force_refetch and self.data_path.exists():\n    98→            print(f\"Loading data from {self.data_path}\", flush=True)\n    99→            df = pd.read_csv(self.data_path, parse_dates=[\"open_time\"])\n   100→        else:\n   101→            print(\"Fetching fresh data from Binance...\", flush=True)\n   102→            df = fetch_and_save_historical(\n   103→                symbol=DataConfig.SYMBOL,\n   104→                interval=DataConfig.INTERVAL,\n   105→                start_date=DataConfig.START_DATE,\n   106→                filepath=str(self.data_path)\n   107→            )\n   108→\n   109→        if df.empty:\n   110→            raise ValueError(\"No data available\")\n   111→\n   112→        print(f\"Loaded {len(df)} rows of data\", flush=True)\n   113→        print(f\"Date range: {df['open_time'].iloc[0]} to {df['open_time'].iloc[-1]}\", flush=True)\n   114→        return df\n   115→\n   116→    def prepare_features(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:\n   117→        \"\"\"\n   118→        Prepare feature matrix X and target y.\n   119→        \"\"\"\n   120→        print(\"Preparing features...\", flush=True)\n   121→\n   122→        # Clean data\n   123→        df = clean_data(df)\n   124→\n   125→        # Create target (next 15-minute direction)\n   126→        df = create_target(df, forward_periods=1)\n   127→\n   128→        # Generate horizon ensemble features (these will be added as extra columns)\n   129→        print(\"  Generating horizon features...\", flush=True)\n   130→        horizon_features = generate_horizon_features(df, FeatureConfig.HORIZONS)\n   131→\n   132→        # Merge horizon features into df\n   133→        df = df.merge(horizon_features, on=\"open_time\", how=\"left\")\n   134→\n   135→        # Drop rows with NaN in target\n   136→        df = df.dropna(subset=[\"target\"])\n   137→\n   138→        # Forward fill any remaining NaNs\n   139→        df = df.ffill().dropna()\n   140→\n   141→        print(f\"Prepared {len(df)} samples with {len(df.columns)} columns\", flush=True)\n   142→        self.feature_names = [\n   143→            col for col in df.columns\n   144→            if col not in [\n   145→                \"open_time\", \"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\",\n   146→                \"quote_volume\", \"trades_count\", \"future_close\", \"target\"\n   147→            ]\n   148→        ]\n   149→\n   150→        print(f\"Feature count: {len(self.feature_names)}\", flush=True)\n   151→        return df\n   152→\n   153→    def evolve_population(\n   154→        self,\n   155→        X_train: pd.DataFrame,\n   156→        y_train: pd.Series,\n   157→        generations: int = ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION\n   158→    ) -> Population:\n   159→        \"\"\"\n   160→        Evolve a population of models.\n   161→        \"\"\"\n   162→        print(f\"Evolving population (input_dim={X_train.shape[1]})...\", flush=True)\n   163→\n   164→        pop = Population(\n   165→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   166→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   167→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   168→            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n   169→            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n   170→        )\n   171→\n   172→        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n   173→\n   174→        for gen in range(generations):\n   175→            print(f\"  Generation {gen + 1}/{generations}\", flush=True)\n   176→\n   177→            # Evaluate all individuals\n   178→            for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   179→                try:\n   180→                    print(f\"    Training individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   181→                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   182→                    proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X_train)\n   183→                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   184→                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   185→\n   186→                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n   187→                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n   188→                    print(f\"      -> fitness={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   189→                except Exception as e:\n   190→                    print(f\"      -> training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   191→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   192→\n   193→            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n   194→            if gen < generations - 1:\n   195→                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n   196→                pop.evolve()\n   197→\n   198→            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   199→            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   200→\n   201→        return pop\n   202→\n   203→    def _log_feature_importances(self, ind) -> None:\n   204→        \"\"\"Log top feature importances from a Random Forest model.\"\"\"\n   205→        if ind is None:\n   206→            return\n   207→        try:\n   208→            if hasattr(ind.model, 'model') and hasattr(ind.model.model, 'feature_importances_'):\n   209→                importances = ind.model.model.feature_importances_\n   210→                n = min(len(importances), len(self.feature_names))\n   211→                feature_imp = pd.Series(importances[:n], index=self.feature_names[:n])\n   212→                top10 = feature_imp.nlargest(10)\n   213→                print(\"\\nTop 10 feature importances:\", flush=True)\n   214→                for fname, imp in top10.items():\n   215→                    print(f\"  {fname}: {imp:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   216→        except Exception:\n   217→            pass\n   218→\n   219→    def _run_fold(self, train_df: pd.DataFrame, valid_df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[Dict]:\n   220→        \"\"\"Run a single fold of walk-forward validation. Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n   221→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   222→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   223→        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n   224→        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n   225→        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n   226→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   227→\n   228→        # Train fresh population on this fold's training data\n   229→        pop = Population(\n   230→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   231→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   232→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   233→            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n   234→            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n   235→        )\n   236→        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n   237→\n   238→        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n   239→            for ind in pop.individuals:\n   240→                try:\n   241→                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   242→                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   243→                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   244→                except Exception as e:\n   245→                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   246→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   247→            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n   248→                pop.evolve()\n   249→            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   250→            print(f\"    Gen {gen+1}: best_train_fitness={best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   251→\n   252→        # Re-score on validation set using profit_factor\n   253→        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   254→            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n   255→                continue\n   256→            try:\n   257→                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n   258→                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n   259→                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n   260→                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n   261→                self.trader.run(signals_ind, valid_ohlc)\n   262→                ind.fitness = self.trader.metrics.get('profit_factor', 0.0)\n   263→                ind.validation_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n   264→                print(f\"  Model {i+1}: profit_factor={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   265→            except Exception as e:\n   266→                print(f\"  Rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   267→                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   268→\n   269→        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n   270→        self._log_feature_importances(top_models[0] if top_models else None)\n   271→\n   272→        # Generate consensus signals\n   273→        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n   274→            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n   275→            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n   276→        )\n   277→        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n   278→\n   279→        # Run simulator\n   280→        self.trader.run(signals, valid_ohlc)\n   281→        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n   282→\n   283→        # Directional accuracy\n   284→        mask = (signals != -1) & y_valid.notna()\n   285→        if mask.any():\n   286→            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n   287→        else:\n   288→            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n   289→\n   290→        print(f\"Fold result: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, \"\n   291→              f\"trades={metrics.get('n_trades', 0)}, sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.3f}\", flush=True)\n   292→        return metrics\n   293→\n   294→    def run_walk_forward(\n   295→        self,\n   296→        df: pd.DataFrame\n   297→    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n   298→        \"\"\"\n   299→        Run 2-fold walk-forward validation with non-overlapping validation windows.\n   300→        Fold 1 (earlier): validates on [T-2v, T-v]; Fold 2 (latest): validates on [T-v, T].\n   301→        Returns weighted-average metrics across folds for robust OOS estimation.\n   302→        \"\"\"\n   303→        print(\"Running multi-fold walk-forward validation...\", flush=True)\n   304→\n   305→        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n   306→        val_rows = int(ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS * 24 * 60 / 15)\n   307→        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n   308→\n   309→        if total_rows < val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   310→            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward.\", flush=True)\n   311→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   312→\n   313→        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n   314→        n_folds = 1\n   315→        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   316→            n_folds = 2\n   317→        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   318→            n_folds = 3\n   319→\n   320→        fold_metrics = []\n   321→        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n   322→            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n   323→            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n   324→            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n   325→\n   326→            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   327→                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n   328→                continue\n   329→\n   330→            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n   331→            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n   332→\n   333→            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   334→                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   335→\n   336→            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n   337→\n   338→            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n   339→            if m:\n   340→                fold_metrics.append(m)\n   341→\n   342→        if not fold_metrics:\n   343→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   344→\n   345→        n = len(fold_metrics)\n   346→        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n   347→\n   348→        if total_trades == 0:\n   349→            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n   350→            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n   351→            return combined\n   352→\n   353→        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n   354→        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n   355→        combined = {\n   356→            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n   357→            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   358→            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   359→            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   360→            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   361→            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   362→            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n   363→            \"n_folds\": n,\n   364→        }\n   365→\n   366→        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n   367→              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n   368→              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n   369→        return combined\n   370→\n   371→    def train_best_models(\n   372→        self,\n   373→        df: pd.DataFrame,\n   374→        population: Population,\n   375→        horizon_data: dict = None\n   376→    ):\n   377→        \"\"\"\n   378→        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n   379→        \"\"\"\n   380→        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n   381→\n   382→        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n   383→        recent_days = 60\n   384→        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n   385→        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n   386→        print(f\"Recent training data: {len(recent_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n   387→\n   388→        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n   389→        y_recent = recent_df[\"target\"]\n   390→\n   391→        # Get top models\n   392→        top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE + 2)\n   393→        print(f\"Selected {len(top_models)} top models for retraining\", flush=True)\n   394→\n   395→        # Retrain on full recent data\n   396→        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n   397→            try:\n   398→                print(f\"  Retraining model {i+1}/{len(top_models)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   399→                ind.model.fit(X_recent, y_recent)\n   400→                print(f\"    Done\", flush=True)\n   401→            except Exception as e:\n   402→                print(f\"  Failed to train {ind.model_type}: {e}\", flush=True)\n   403→\n   404→        # Train horizon ensemble if not provided and if we have multiple horizons\n   405→        if horizon_data is None:\n   406→            horizon_data = {}\n   407→            horizons_to_train = [h for h in FeatureConfig.HORIZONS.keys() if h != \"15m\"]\n   408→            if horizons_to_train:\n   409→                print(f\"Training horizon ensemble for {len(horizons_to_train)} horizons...\", flush=True)\n   410→                for h_name in horizons_to_train:\n   411→                    factor = FeatureConfig.HORIZONS[h_name]\n   412→                    print(f\"  Horizon {h_name} (factor={factor})\", flush=True)\n   413→                    from .data.processor import resample_to_horizon\n   414→                    # Use correct horizon minutes: factor * 15 minutes\n   415→                    horizon_minutes = factor * 15\n   416→                    df_horizon = resample_to_horizon(recent_df, horizon_minutes, factor)\n   417→                    print(f\"    Resampled to {len(df_horizon)} rows\", flush=True)\n   418→                    if len(df_horizon) > 100:\n   419→                        df_horizon = create_target(df_horizon, forward_periods=1)\n   420→                        df_horizon = add_technical_indicators(df_horizon)\n   421→                        df_horizon = add_regime_features(df_horizon)\n   422→                        df_horizon = df_horizon.dropna()\n   423→                        print(f\"    Prepared {len(df_horizon)} samples with {len(df_horizon.columns)} features\", flush=True)\n   424→                        horizon_data[h_name] = df_horizon\n   425→                self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n   426→                print(\"Horizon ensemble training complete\", flush=True)\n   427→            else:\n   428→                print(\"No additional horizons to train (HORIZONS only includes 15m)\", flush=True)\n   429→        else:\n   430→            self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n   431→\n   432→        self.main_population = population\n   433→        self.top_models = top_models\n   434→\n   435→    def generate_current_signals(\n   436→        self,\n   437→        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n   438→        use_horizon: bool = True\n   439→    ) -> pd.Series:\n   440→        \"\"\"\n   441→        Generate trading signals for the most recent data points.\n   442→        \"\"\"\n   443→        if self.top_models is None:\n   444→            raise RuntimeError(\"Models not trained. Call train_best_models first.\")\n   445→\n   446→        signals = self.consensus_gate.decide(self.top_models, current_features)\n   447→        return signals\n   448→\n   449→    def run_online_step(self, new_data: pd.DataFrame = None):\n   450→        \"\"\"\n   451→        Execute one iteration of the online evolution loop.\n   452→\n   453→        This is the main step method called repeatedly by Arbos.\n   454→        \"\"\"\n   455→        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n   456→        print(\"RUNNING ONLINE STEP\", flush=True)\n   457→        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n   458→\n   459→        # 1. Load/fetch latest data\n   460→        if new_data is None:\n   461→            df = self.load_or_fetch_data()\n   462→        else:\n   463→            df = new_data\n   464→\n   465→        # 2. For online operation, limit to most recent N days to bound runtime\n   466→        if ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS is not None:\n   467→            cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS)\n   468→            df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff].copy()\n   469→            print(f\"Online mode: limited data to last {ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS} days ({len(df)} rows)\", flush=True)\n   470→\n   471→        # 3. Prepare features\n   472→        print(\"[main] Starting feature preparation...\", flush=True)\n   473→        df = self.prepare_features(df)\n   474→        print(f\"[main] Feature preparation complete: {len(df)} rows, {len(self.feature_names)} features\", flush=True)\n   475→\n   476→        # 3. Split into recent data for training and current for prediction\n   477→        # Use last 30 days for training, current for signal generation\n   478→        recent_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=30)\n   479→        train_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] <= recent_cutoff].copy()\n   480→        current_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] > recent_cutoff].copy()\n   481→\n   482→        # Limit training samples to control memory/time (use most recent samples)\n   483→        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   484→            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   485→            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n   486→\n   487→        if len(train_df) < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   488→            print(f\"Insufficient training data: {len(train_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n   489→            return None\n   490→\n   491→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   492→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   493→\n   494→        # 4. Evolve population\n   495→        population = self.evolve_population(X_train, y_train, generations=ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION)\n   496→\n   497→        # 5. Walk-forward validation on historical folds (use recent data to limit folds)\n   498→        if ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS is not None:\n   499→            wf_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS)\n   500→            df_wf = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= wf_cutoff].copy()\n   501→            print(f\"Using {len(df_wf)} recent samples for walk-forward validation (max {ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS} days)\", flush=True)\n   502→        else:\n   503→            df_wf = df\n   504→        metrics = self.run_walk_forward(df_wf)\n   505→\n   506→        # Adapt consensus thresholds based on walk-forward metrics\n   507→        self.consensus_gate.adjust_thresholds(metrics)\n   508→\n   509→        # 6. Train best models on full recent data and prepare horizon ensemble\n   510→        self.train_best_models(df, population)\n   511→\n   512→        # 7.      symbol=DataConfig.SYMBOL,\n                interval=DataConfig.INTERVAL,\n                start_date=DataConfig.START_DATE,\n                filepath=str(self.data_path)\n            )\n\n {df['open_time'].iloc[-1]}\", flush=True)\n        return df\n\n    def prepare_features(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        \"\"\"\n        Prepare feature matrix X and target y.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Preparing features...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Clean data\n        df = clean_data(df)\n\n        # Create target (next 15-minute direction)\n        df = horizon_features = generate_horizon_features(df, FeatureConfig.HORIZONS)\n\n        # Merge horizon features into df\n        df = df.merge(horizon_features, on=\"open_time\", how=\"left\")\n\n        # Drop rows with NaN in target\n        df = df.dropna(subset=[\"target\"])\n\n        # Forward fill any remaining NaNs\n        df = df.ffill().dropna()\n\n        print(f\"Prepared {len(df)} {len(self.feature_names)}\", flush=True)\n        return df\n\n    def evolve_population(\n        self,\n        X_train: pd.DataFrame,\n        y_train: pd.Series,\n        generations: int = ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION\n    ) -> Population:\n        \"\"\"\n        Evolve a population of models.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(f\"Evolving population (input_dim={X_train.shape[1]})...\", flush=True)\n\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(generations):\n            print(f\"  Generation {gen + 1}/{generations}\", flush=True)\n\n            # Evaluate all individuals\n            for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n                try:\n                    print(f\"    Training individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n\n                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n                    print(f\"      -> fitness={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"      -> training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n            if gen < generations - 1:\n                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n                pop.evolve()\n\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        return pop\n\n    def _log_feature_importances(self, ind) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Log top feature importances from a Random Forest model.\"\"\"\n        if ind is None:\n            return\n        try:\n            if hasattr(ind.model, 'model') and hasattr(ind.model.model, 'feature_importances_'):\n                importances = ind.model.model.feature_importances_\n                n = min(len(importances), len(self.feature_names))\n                feature_imp = pd.Series(importances[:n], index=self.feature_names[:n])\n                top10 = feature_imp.nlargest(10)\n                print(\"\\nTop 10 feature importances:\", flush=True)\n                for fname, imp in top10.items():\n                    print(f\"  {fname}: {imp:.4f}\", flush=True)\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n\n    def _run_fold(self, train_df: pd.DataFrame, valid_df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Run a single fold of walk-forward validation. Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Train fresh population on this fold's training data\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n                pop.evolve()\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Gen {gen+1}: best_train_fitness={best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        # Re-score on validation set using profit_factor\n        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n                continue\n            try:\n                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n                self.trader.run(signals_ind, valid_ohlc)\n                ind.fitness = self.trader.metrics.get('profit_factor', 0.0)\n                ind.validation_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n                print(f\"  Model {i+1}: profit_factor={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n        self._log_feature_importances(top_models[0] if top_models else None)\n\n        # Generate consensus signals\n        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n        )\n        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n\n        # Run simulator\n        self.trader.run(signals, valid_ohlc)\n        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n\n        # Directional accuracy\n        mask = (signals != -1) & y_valid.notna()\n        if mask.any():\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n        else:\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n\n        print(f\"Fold result: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, \"\n              f\"trades={metrics.get('n_trades', 0)}, sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.3f}\", flush=True)\n        return metrics\n\n    def run_walk_forward(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run 2-fold walk-forward validation with non-overlapping validation windows.\n        Fold 1 (earlier): validates on [T-2v, T-v]; Fold 2 (latest): validates on [T-v, T].\n        Returns weighted-average metrics across folds for robust OOS estimation.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running multi-fold walk-forward validation...\", flush=True)\n\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n        val_rows = int(ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS * 24 * 60 / 15)\n        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n\n        if total_rows < val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward.\", flush=True)\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n        n_folds = 1\n        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 2\n        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 3\n\n        fold_metrics = []\n        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n\n            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n                continue\n\n            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n\n            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n\n            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n\n            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n            if m:\n                fold_metrics.append(m)\n\n        if not fold_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        n = len(fold_metrics)\n        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n\n        if total_trades == 0:\n            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n            return combined\n\n        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n        combined = {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n            \"n_folds\": n,\n        }\n\n        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n        return combined\n\n    def train_best_models(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population,\n        horizon_data: dict = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n        recent_days = 60\n        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n        print(f\"Recent training data: {len(recent_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n\n        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_recent = recent_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Get top models\n        top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE + 2)\n        print(f\"Selected {len(top_models)} top models for retraining\", flush=True)\n\n        # Retrain on full recent data\n        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Retraining model {i+1}/{len(top_models)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                ind.model.fit(X_recent, y_recent)\n                print(f\"    Done\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Failed to train {ind.model_type}: {e}\", flush=True)\n\n        # Train horizon ensemble if not provided and if we have multiple horizons\n        if horizon_data is None:\n            horizon_data = {}\n            horizons_to_train = [h for h in FeatureConfig.HORIZONS.keys() if h != \"15m\"]\n            if horizons_to_train:\n                print(f\"Training horizon ensemble for {len(horizons_to_train)} horizons...\", flush=True)\n                for h_name in horizons_to_train:\n                    factor = FeatureConfig.HORIZONS[h_name]\n                    print(f\"  Horizon {h_name} (factor={factor})\", flush=True)\n                    from .data.processor import resample_to_horizon\n                    # Use correct horizon minutes: factor * 15 minutes\n                    horizon_minutes = factor * 15\n                    df_horizon = resample_to_horizon(recent_df, horizon_minutes, factor)\n                    print(f\"    Resampled to {len(df_horizon)} rows\", flush=True)\n                    if len(df_horizon) > 100:\n                        df_horizon = create_target(df_horizon, forward_periods=1)\n                        df_horizon = add_technical_indicators(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = add_regime_features(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = df_horizon.dropna()\n                        print(f\"    Prepared {len(df_horizon)} samples with {len(df_horizon.columns)} features\", flush=True)\n                        horizon_data[h_name] = df_horizon\n                self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n                print(\"Horizon ensemble training complete\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                print(\"No additional horizons to train (HORIZONS only includes 15m)\", flush=True)\n        else:\n            self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n\n        self.main_population = population\n        self.top_models = top_models\n\n    def generate_current_signals(\n        self,\n        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n        use_horizon: bool = True\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate trading signals for the most recent data points.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.top_models is None:\n            raise RuntimeError(\"Models not trained. Call train_best_models first.\")\n\n        signals = self.consensus_gate.decide(self.top_models, current_features)\n        return signals\n\n    def run_online_step(self, new_data: pd.DataFrame = None):\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute one iteration of the online evolution loop.\n\n        This is the main step method called repeatedly by Arbos.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n        print(\"RUNNING ONLINE STEP\", flush=True)\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n\n        # 1. Load/fetch latest data\n        if new_data is None:\n            df = self.load_or_fetch_data()\n        else:\n            df = new_data\n\n        # 2. \"\"\"\n        Compute composite fitness score.\n\n        Fitness = w1*accuracy + w2*bet_ratio + w3*sharpe - w4*drawdown\n        where bet_ratio = (bets_per_month / target_bets) capped at 1\n )\n\n    def _crossover(self, parent1: Individual, parent2: Individual) -> Individual:\n        \"\"\"Crossover between two parents (blend or swap).\"\"\"\n        if random.random() > self.crossover_rate:\n            return parent1\n\n        # Simple parameter averaging or swap for same model type\n        if parent1.model_type != parent2.model_type:\n            return
